Each player starts with sixteen pieces: eight pawns, two knights, two bishops, two rooks, one queen and one king. The goal of the game is for each player to try and checkmate the king of the opponent. Checkmate is a threat ('check') to the opposing king which no move can stop. It ends the game.\r\nDuring the game the two opponents take turns to move one of their pieces to a different square of the board. One player ('White') has pieces of a light color; the other player ('Black') has pieces of a dark color. There are rules about how pieces move, and about taking the opponent's pieces off the board. The player with white pieces always makes the first move. Because of this, White has a small advantage, and wins more often than Black in tournament games.\r\nDeveloping Chess strategy and improving your Chess skill! Besides, AX-ZIP Extractor is simple and convenient file manager.\r\n\r\nMain Features\r\n\r\nExtraction from ZIP, CAB, RAR, JAR, XAP, GZIP, BZIP2, XZ, TAR and 7Z archives.\r\nExtraction from ISO images (ISO 9660 and ISO 13346 \"UDF\").\r\nSimultaneous work with several archives.\r\nOne drag extraction of files from archive.\r\nSearch of archives and files within the archives.\r\nBookmarks for archives and files in the archives.\r\nSupport of cloud drives and special folders.\r\nSupport of main file manager functions.\r\nSupport of drag and drop technology.\r\nDisplay of archive structure as a tree.\r\nFamiliar Explorer-like user interface.\r\n\r\nOverview\r\n\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor utility views ZIP archives and archives of other types as folders containing folders and files whose structure is shown as a tree. Thus the root folder of archive will be displayed as an icon associated with archives of that type.\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor working space is made up of two windows - Archive Browser and File Browser.\r\nArchive Browser contains a tree representing the structure of disks, folders and archives - files with extension of supported archive types. To open archive one should simply click \"+\" sign situated on the left of archive name.\r\nFile Browser shows full structure of disks, folders and files.\r\nAll operations in AX-ZIP Extractor concerning archive management involve dragging of items from one window to the other.\r\n\r\nWhat's New in Version 4.4\r\n\r\nNew engine for extracting files from ZIP archives.\r\nAdded support of LZMA compression method for ZIP archives.\r\nExtraction from XZ archives.\r\nExtraction from XZ compressed TAR archives.\r\nAdded support of custom archives (based on zip).\r\nAdded detection of insertion or removal of drives (such as USB flash drives).\r\nSupport of cloud drive iCloud Drive.\r\nSupport of special folder Desktop.\r\nThe performance of some operations is
